This algorithm is known in mathematics as the Sieve of Eratosthenes--inherent in sruti verses of Vedas<br /><br />In mathematics, the sieve of Eratosthenes one of a number of prime number sieves, is a simple, ancient algorithm for finding all prime numbers up to any given limit.<br /><br />It does so by iteratively marking as composite, i.e., not prime, the multiples of each prime, starting with the multiples of 2. The multiples of a given prime are generated starting from that prime, as a sequence of numbers with the same difference, equal to that prime, between consecutive numbers.<br /><br />This is the sieve's key distinction from using trial division to sequentially test each candidate number for divisibility by each prime.<br /><br />MY REVELATIONS NOW JUMP TO&nbsp;<span style=\"color: red; <br />\n<br />\nTheir historians portrayed Britain as a honourable country. The British white man in India was full of fair play and justice--BLAH BLAH.<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LF-TwdT0q8A/T81Jokwn2eI/AAAAAAAAL5g/d7NXI4siy7g/s1600/imagesCATBG5RY.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-LF-TwdT0q8A/T81Jokwn2eI/AAAAAAAAL5g/d7NXI4siy7g/s1600/imagesCATBG5RY.jpg\" height=\"400\" width=\"291\" /></a></div>\n<br />\nIn the first movie Pazhassi Raja committed suicide by swallowing his diamond ring. Such a coward he was, right?&nbsp;&nbsp; <br />\n<br />\nHere was a king who did NOT bow down to Hyder Ali , Tipu Sultan and the British-- a&nbsp;great fighter who used guerrilla commando methods with a small band of loyal archers and swordsmen against a superior army .<br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; He is the character portrayed by Jagathi Sreekumar.<br />\n<br />\nBaber cremated the king&nbsp;the same day.<br />\n<br />\n. <br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://1.bp.blogspot.com/-VHYmxwIguFE/T81KAv2SnEI/AAAAAAAAL54/-nRKQlZ5PM8/s1600/340px-Kerala_in_15th_century.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; Grace and peace!!</em><br />\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<object class=\"BLOGGER-youtube-video\" classid=\"clsid:D27CDB6E-AE6D-11cf-96B8-444553540000\" codebase=\"http://download.macromedia.com/pub/shockwave/cabs/flash/swflash.cab#version=6,0,40,0\" data-thumbnail-src=\"http://1.gvt0.com/vi/Jr5wT3CFwmk/0.jpg\" height=\"266\" width=\"320\"><param name=\"movie\" value=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/Jr5wT3CFwmk&fs=1&source=uds\" />\n\n<param name=\"bgcolor\" value=\"#FFFFFF\" />\n\n<param name=\"allowFullScreen\" value=\"true\" />\n\n<embed width=\"320\" height=\"266\"  src=\"http://www.youtube.com/v/Jr5wT3CFwmk&fs=1&source=uds\" type=\"application/x-shockwave-flash\" allowfullscreen=\"true\"></embed></object></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BbVHV1p3EBI/T8mmX_EwkoI/AAAAAAAALx8/-NLadloAuIc/s1600/VADAKAYIL2.JPG\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-BbVHV1p3EBI/T8mmX_EwkoI/AAAAAAAALx8/-NLadloAuIc/s320/VADAKAYIL2.JPG\" height=\"239\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<br />\nCAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<br />\n..<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br />\n<br /></div>\n", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. Ajit Vadakayil", "url": "https://www.blogger.com/profile/14410812789424637654", "image": {"url": "//4.bp.blogspot.com/-QSnd-Z8F7Kc/XFtPudWdwlI/AAAAAAABfq4/vxrkFOO7Iu8Mf6-OaPgw6FPpRDSmMgLdgCK4BGAYYCw/s35/capt%25252BajitC%25252Bvadakayil.JPG"}}, "replies": {"totalItems": "24", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/338755730291203682/comments"}}, {"kind": "blogger#post", "id": "5317242410589878481", "blog": {"id": "3564735312144269387"}, "published": "2012-06-02T09:01:00+05:30", "updated": "2012-06-02T09:01:21+05:30", "etag": "\"iHf3yWDE_geBgZ8U7rgZ_xuTeAQ/dGltZXN0YW1wOiAxMzM4NjA3ODgxOTMzCm9mZnNldDogMTk4MDAwMDAK\"", "url": "http://ajitvadakayil.blogspot.com/2012/06/pipeline-cleaning-and-blowing-on.html", "selfLink": "https://www.googleapis.com/blogger/v3/blogs/3564735312144269387/posts/5317242410589878481", "title": "PIPELINE CLEANING AND BLOWING ON CHEMICAL TANKERS - CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL", "content": "<div dir=\"ltr\" style=\"text-align: left;\" trbidi=\"on\">\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Nou1H3gd5L4/T8mHj3kA51I/AAAAAAAALtA/BZHtS5UqumQ/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://3.bp.blogspot.com/-Nou1H3gd5L4/T8mHj3kA51I/AAAAAAAALtA/BZHtS5UqumQ/s1600/imagesCA0O0WVC.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><strong><span style=\"font-size: large;\"><span style=\"color: red;\">PIPELINE CLEANING AND BLOWING\nON CHEMICAL TANKERS - CAPT AJIT VADAKAYIL<o:p></o:p></span></span></strong></span></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OONsD3AUeu4/T8mIUSTKACI/AAAAAAAALtI/Aqe0jDfkIEI/s1600/SAM_4762.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"400\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-OONsD3AUeu4/T8mIUSTKACI/AAAAAAAALtI/Aqe0jDfkIEI/s400/SAM_4762.jpg\" width=\"297\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Always ensure the\nmedium used for blowing a pipeline is suited for the chemical inside.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">While line clearing it\nis important to listen , rather than checking static pressure on the gauges. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A large 6 inch diameter\npipeline when blown uphill against the trim will cause the air to skim over the\ncargo inside the pipeline , as air tends to find and remains at highest level\nand liquid at the lowest level. This is why super stripping is done with small diameter\n1.5 inch pipelines where a steady air blow will suffice. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">With large diameter\npipelines it is necessary to pressurize the pipeline and release suddenly , to\nsquirt the liquid off. This is done many times till the flow of liquid past the\nopening valve is no longer heard or detected.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Submarine terminals for\nannex 1 CPP do not allow chemical tankers to blow air , as air inside the\nsubmerged hose can break it off its underwater moorings and damage it. In such\ncases water plug must be given . It is necessary to be prepared for this in\nadvance.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Lines used for cargo\noperations must be cleared and pressure released to prevent solidification, polymerization,\npitting and danger to personnel connecting/ disconnecting blanks and hoses or\ntaking samples.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">After cargo work is\nover the ships crew must clear the pipelines. A free flowing cargo like\nsulphuric acid if allowed to slosh between port and stbd manifolds at sea\nduring rolling , can damage the butterfly valve discs. Hence it is important to\nclear dead ends too . Heated cargoes will freeze and cause delays. Line\nclearance must be planned well.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Many off specification\n\"First foots\" have resulted from contaminates remaining in the ships\ncargo line system. It is therefore most important that all aspects of line\ncleaning are included in the ship's tank cleaning program and are clearly\ndefined.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\"><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During tank washing, a\npositive line pressure should be maintained to ensure that all surfaces of the\nline are washed. The manifold valves should be adjusted to maintain the\npositive pressure.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Crossover manifold, one\nmust ensure that both sides of the manifold are washed out simultaneously with\nthe tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If fitted, drop lines,\nrestricted gauging pipes and stripping lines must be washed simultaneously with\nthe tank.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">If any of the valves\nfitted in the cargo line have plugs, same should be removed. All such valves\nshould be opened and closed at regular intervals. This assists the wash water\nin flushing the valve face and casing.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">All drain cocks in the\nline should have the dust caps off, and the drain cocks flushed at regular\nintervals.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Blind flanges must be\nloosened at the end of tank washing to ensure proper cleaning.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Tank vent lines must be\ncleaned out during the rough washing as required.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">All vapor return lines\nand associated equipment must be thoroughly cleaned and dried.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">After completion of\ntank washing, if circumstances permit: all valves, plugs and drains should be\nleft in the open position. This allows the line(s) to drain and assists in\ndrying.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The tank inspection,\nafter washing, must include all lines and fittings associated with the tank as\noutlined in \"Tank inspection.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When a secondary\ncleaning method is found necessary, the same cleaning method must also be\napplied to all tank associated piping, including vapor return equipment.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">A program for final\ntank preparation can now be carried out (i.e.) fresh water rinsing the tank(s),\nsteaming the cargo lines, vent lines, drop lines, stripping lines, restricted\ngauge pipes and any other fittings required for such preparation.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The tanks should be\nfresh water rinsed before line steaming commences.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Line steaming: Check\nthe steam condensate for color and chlorides; if any contaminants found:\n\"clear the system.\"<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Connect suitable size\nsteam hoses to each side of the manifold of the line to be steamed. Steam the\nline to the pump stack drain valve, with the pump stack cargo line valve\ninitially closed.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">During the line\nsteaming, the steam pressure must be sufficient to ensure a flow of steam at\nthe pump stack drain valve outlet and not just condensate.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">All valves and drain\nvalves including the pump stack valve should be opened and closed at regular\nintervals during the line steaming. This assists in removing any entrapped\nresidues and dissolves chloride salts left by the sea water washing. To prevent\ndamage to seals, packings, etc., never force a valve which is heated to open or\nclose. The coefficient of expansion of the seal is different from that of the\ncasing and if force is used, the seal can be damaged. When a valve does not\nproperly function when heated, allow the valve to cool prior to opening or\nclosing.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">With difficult cargo ( like black heavy furnace oil) \nresidue or line design, using a steam injector fitted to the manifold and\ninjecting 5 liters of toluene has given very good results.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The steam should be\nsampled at regular intervals at the pump stack drain valve outlet and\ncondensate checked for contaminants. This will give an indication that the\nsteaming has achieved the cleanliness<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;\n</span>required or that further cleaning and/or steaming is required.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Vent lines must always\nbe fresh water rinsed and/or steamed upon completion of tank washing.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When steaming vent\nlines, ensure that the steam is coming out both pressure and vacuum ends of the\nline, open and close drain valves vapor return connections at regular\nintervals, and ensure a positive steam flow at these outlets.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Drop and stripping\nlines should be steamed simultaneously when steaming cargo lines. Line steaming\nmust be closely monitored to ensure that line and valve seals and packing are\nnot damaged by excessive heat. Do not use excessive force to open or close a\nvalve which is heated.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">For draining cargo\nline\u2014the chief officer must be PERSONALLY aware of the 3 D<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>configuration of pipelines.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Deck airline must\nalways be drained from the lowest position..<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Line blowing must\nalways be discussed in the pre-loading meeting and agreement put down in\nwriting. To be done with air/ steam/ nitrogen. Ensure cargo does not enter the\nair/ steam/ nitrogen line.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Line\nBlowing<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Line blowing will be\ncarried out using air or Nitrogen as required according to<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the cargo characteristics. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Most terminals will\nwant to clear the shore line and hose all the way to the<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>ships tank to expedite completion. Often the\nshore will clear their own lines by<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>pigging then blowing from the dock line.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When clearing lines\nfrom the shore tanks a large volume of air will be used<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and the effect of this air on the tank levels\nmust be considered . Hence preferably blow the shore lines into one single\nslack tank , and this tank must be ullaged last to allow the cargo to settle\ndown. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Air will skim through\nthe big pipelines much faster than liquid and<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>bubbles rising from the bottom drop line will expand very quickly having\na<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>considerable effect on the levels\nwithin the tank.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Line blowing into tanks\nthat are loaded to 98% (or close to 98%) should<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>therefore be avoided wherever possible.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>Estimate the line content of shore hose and ships line to the cargo tank<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<b style=\"mso-bidi-font-weight: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Blow\nProcedure <o:p></o:p></span></b></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<i style=\"mso-bidi-font-style: normal;\"><span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Note:\nIt must be understood that large dia pipelines will cause the air to skim on\ntop while the liquid will remain at the bottom, as it always finds the highest\npoint and liquid always finds the lowest point. That is why super strip lines\nare small dia pipelines.<o:p></o:p></span></i></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Manifold valve\nopen.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Drop line valve\nclosed.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Shore slowly builds up\npressure in the shore line and hose. (The pressure<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>should not<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;\n</span>exceed<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>80% of the ship\u2019s lines\nMWP).<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Watch pressure increase\nat the pressure gauge fitted outside the manifold<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>valve.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;\n</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Slowly open dropline\nvalve, about 10% should be enough no more than<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>20%.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Listen for the sound of\ncargo draining into tank.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When you hear air\nbubbling into the tank it is time to close the drop valve. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">First foot sample fails\nif line cleaning is not OK.&nbsp;<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;(<em>That is why you must take the manifold first foot sample at loadport with manifold valve shut as far as possible</em> ). </span>Throttle\nmanifold valves sufficiently so that the lines are chock-a-block with water and\ndischg to annex 2 overboard from both the sides. Also flush<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>drops, MMC pipes, superstrip lines, vent\nlines , drain cocks etc. After completion of steaming<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>keep all valves , plugs<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and drains open to dry. Use steam to flush PV\nstack.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">When flushing lines\noperate the valves open/ shut a couple of times to clean out the valves. <span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;</span><o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before commencing\ndischarge arrangements are to be agreed for the blowing<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>back of cargo. Once agreed there must be no\ndeviation form the agreed blow back procedure without further discussion and\nanother written agreement. After the blow crack open the drop valve and the\ndischarge valve to release air pressure from the<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>deck cargo line.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">PPE and goggles, face\nshield must be worn by crew involves in line blowing. Good communications are a\nmust. Any personnel not involved must clear the area. Risk assessment must be\ndone for aggressive , toxic and carcinogenic cargoes.<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">Before arrival\ndischarge port with high MP cargoes it is a good practise to tap with a spanner\n( for a clear ring )<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>the jetty side of\nthe manifold<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>and<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>low areas of<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp;\n</span>dischg delivery pipelines to check if the lines are clear, so that\nyou<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>have sufficient reaction time if\nsomething needs to be done to clear frozen part of lines.<span style=\"mso-spacerun: yes;\">&nbsp; </span>If the lines are frozen the tap will cause a\ndull thunk. <o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">The vent systems are as\nimportant for cargo<o:p></o:p></span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">work as the liquid\nlines. Heated high MP cargo fumes can reduce the dia of the vent cooled by icy\nwinds, which then must be cleared by steam.</span></div>\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_85EOcVTL1Y/T8mHbGqP0-I/AAAAAAAALs4/SqGIKrJLUdI/s1600/VADAKAYIL3.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" height=\"283\" src=\"http://2.bp.blogspot.com/-_85EOcVTL1Y/T8mHbGqP0-I/AAAAAAAALs4/SqGIKrJLUdI/s320/VADAKAYIL3.jpg\" width=\"320\" /></a></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<span style=\"font-family: &quot;Times New Roman&quot;,&quot;serif&quot;; font-size: 12pt; line-height: 150%;\">-------CAPT AJIT\nVADAKAYIL ( 29 YEARS IN COMMAND )</span></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n<br />\n<div class=\"MsoNormal\" style=\"line-height: 150%; margin: 0in 0in 10pt;\">\n<br /></div>\n</div>", "author": {"id": "14410812789424637654", "displayName": "Capt. It is best done in the morning after emptying your bowels on a\nempty stomach.<o:p></o:p></div>\n<br />\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\nThough the Vedic Maharishis have NOT advises this,\nI would recommend you to lightly plug your ears with cotton balls. Also the HUMMMMMMM will\nresonate your pineal gland. </div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div class=\"separator\" style=\"clear: both; text-align: center;\">\n<a href=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6MujS5M58Kg/T8dIc9FVDCI/AAAAAAAALrI/SIAww4epA5I/s1600/imagesCAJDH797.jpg\" imageanchor=\"1\" style=\"margin-left: 1em; margin-right: 1em;\"><img border=\"0\" src=\"http://4.bp.blogspot.com/-6MujS5M58Kg/T8dIc9FVDCI/AAAAAAAALrI/SIAww4epA5I/s1600/imagesCAJDH797.jpg\" /></a></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<br /></div>\n<div style=\"line-height: 150%;\">\n<span style=\"color: red;\">Try saying MMM without plugging your ears and then\ndo it after plugging your ears-- you will know what I mean.
